        var page_data = {"domain_id":25,"design_id":0,"page_id":0};        (function(){
            var img = new Image();
            var pixel_image_src = '/pix/'+Math.random()+'/report/pixel.gif?type=pageview&domain_id=25&page_id=0&design_id=0&l='+encodeURIComponent(navigator.language)+'&p='+encodeURIComponent(navigator.platform)+'&url='+encodeURIComponent(document.location);

<script>
    var init_page = function() {
        var on_scroll = function() {
            $('.top-news').each(function(){
                if ($(window).scrollTop()*1 > $(this).attr('orig_top')*1 + original_height_news_header*1) {
                    if ($(this).hasClass('fix_news_header')) {
                        return;
                    }
                    $(this).addClass('fix_news_header').css('width', $(this).attr('orig_width')+'px');
                    $(this).css('opacity', 0);
                    $(this).animate({'opacity':'0.85'}, 1000);
                } else {
                    if (! $(this).hasClass('fix_news_header')) {
                        return;
                    }
                    $(this).removeClass('fix_news_header');
                    $(this).css('width', '100%');
                    $(this).css('opacity', 1);
                }
            });
        }
        $('.top-news').removeClass('fix_news_header');
        $('.top-news').css('width', '100%');
        $('.top-news').each(function(){
            $(this).attr('orig_top', $(this).offset().top);
            $(this).attr('orig_width', $(this).width());
        });
        var original_height_news_header = $('.top-news').eq(0).outerHeight();
        on_scroll();
        $(window).scroll(on_scroll);

        var max=0;
        $('.front-step-col').each(function(){
            var h = $(this).height();
            if (h > max) {
                max=h;
            }});
        $('.front-step').css('height', max+'px');
    };

    $(document).ready(function(){
        init_page();
        $(window).resize(init_page);
    });
</script>
